< Text>
I was looking all over for a 2008 Dodge dually long bed in white. Subway had one and they sent pictures of it to my email for me to look it over. I liked it and wanted it so I called them back and we talked. I was going out of the country in a day so I offered to send them 1000$ Non refundable to hold it for me until my return. They agreed and I gave them my cc #. I called them on my return and I arranged a time to get the bed and they suggested that for an additional 100$ they would remove my bed and replace it with their bed and do it all right there while I waited. I worried how I would do what they offered to do in my yard and without a crane and decided for 100$ to let them do the swap. Best $ I ever spent. Once there I also found a rear bumper for the same truck and bought it also. They installed it too. What nice folks. Since then, I have continued to call them for other parts and also for a 12 inch x 12 inch bed floor to patch a hole in another bed that I have. They always seem to come through even with odd or strange requests. I will go nowhere else but to Subway for future parts needs. Thank you Tony for your help and look forward to future purchases with Subway. If only all businesses could be so good to work with!<//Text>

<Date>1620238336884<//Date>< Text>
My husband and I wanted to try something new but were in the mood for garlic noodles. Found this spot on Yelp.

I got the premium bbq combo with garlic noodles and a fried egg. It came in a cute disposable bento box with pickled and steamed veggies. With a slice of pineapple delicious. Everything had great flavor and very filling.
My husband got the chili shrimp and spicy garlic noodles which were also great. We also order the super fruit organic jasmine drink and the organic mango smoothie pearl which this one reminded me of boba but with jellies instead of tapioca balls.

Overall was a great first impression and we will be coming back.</Text>

<user>114378983643185654958<//user><Name>Micah Reich</Name><time>1556944774327</time><rate>5< /rate>< Text>
Food was great, had a ton of flavor. Portions were overly generous. I'm a big dude with a large appetite, was full halfway through my meal. Ordered vermicelli with lemon grass chicken. Came with a jalepeno chutneys, fish sauce, and a salad dressing. All house made with great flavor. The real draw though is I'm a milk tea addict. I got the Ancient Black Fresh Milk Tea. This is some of the best boba tea I've had, maybe the best. I'm not a boba person, usually omit it, just do straight tea brown sugar, or crema. Not with this tea. The boba is stupid fresh with the perfect chewiness to it.  Can't wait to try them again. And yes I would totally stop by just for tea alone. Food is just a bonus to me.</Text>

<Review>Great family park for parties or play days.  Several picnic areas, playground and ballfield. Outdoor half court basketball is unmarked and rough asphalt.  Poles are installed for grass volleyball, bring your own net.  Lots of space to run, play and explore.  My kids enjoy climbing trees, summiting the dirt mounds, and trying to get across to the "island" that is created by seasonal flows in the drainage ditch. Have a hard time not driving down to Monterey for a day or weekend trip and stopping at the Pepper Palace. They have tons of flavors and varieties of hot sauces, salsas, rubs, and more. They sell drinks too in the likelihood you sample something out of your heat range.

I always find one or two bottles to bring home and share, most recent being the Sardine sauce (lol, I just liked the name). $9.95 for a regular sized bottle, kind of a vinegar base with habanero peppers. Really tasty and pretty hot! Stop in and sample some in your in this area!< /text>

< review>
Wonderful park for toddlers and elementary age kids. There is a fenced in area with sand, slides, and swings. There is a splash pad that is open in the summertime and there is an area with a pirate ship for older kids. There is also a basketball court and tennis court and an area with grills and a bathroom. This park can get very busy during the summer and the parking lot is very small. I usually park on the street and walk to the park. The only reason this park doesn‚Äôt get a five star review is because parking can be difficult.<//review>
